route-policy TUZLA-GOOGLE-DENEME-EXPORT
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any DO-NOT-ANNOUNCE-TNAP then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT COGENT IP TRANSIT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^174_') then
    drop
  endif
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^6762_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT TT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^9121_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT INTEROUTE PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^8928_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT Superonline PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^34984_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT VCNO IP TRANSIT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^1273_') then
    drop
  endif
  #Google_Private_Deneme
  #TNAP REJECT
  if community matches-any TIER1-GLOBAL-COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET BIRI PREFIXES
  if community matches-any VFNET_ADANAISG or community matches-any VFNET_ANTALYAISG or community matches-any VFNET_IZMITISG or community matches-any VFNET-ULUS-ODM or community matches-any VFNET-IZMIRHATAYTT or community matches-any VFNET-ANKARA_FTTH or community matches-any VFNET_AFYONISG or community matches-any VFNET_BALIKESIRISG or community matches-any VFNET_MANISAISG or community matches-any VFNET-ANTALYA_FTTH or community matches-any VFNET_ADANAFTTHISG or community matches-any VFNET-IZMIR_FTTH then
    prepend as-path 15924 2
    drop
  endif
  #VODAFONE_MOBILE
  if community matches-any VF-ESY-GGSN or community matches-any VF-ESY-GGSN-GR1 or community matches-any VF-ESY-GGSN-GR2 or community matches-any VF-ESY-Catch_All then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VF-PSK-GGSN or community matches-any VF-PSK-Catch_All or community matches-any VF-ERZ-GGSN or community matches-any VF-SAM-GGSN or community matches-any VF-DYB-GGSN then
    prepend as-path 15924 2
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VF-TZL-GGSN or community matches-any VF-TZL-Catch_All then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VF-GZM-GGSN or community matches-any VF-ANT-GGSN or community matches-any VF-GZM-Catch_All or community matches-any VF-ADN-GGSN or community matches-any VF-ADN-Catch_All then

  endif

  endif

    done
  endif
  if community matches-any Magticom then
    done
  endif

  endif

end-policy
!
route-policy Tuzla-VCNO-IPv6-BGP-Import
  delete community all
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/48
  if destination in Smaller_than_48 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_Unique_Local_Addresses
  if destination in Reject-RFC4193-IPv6 then
    drop
  endif
  #Default
  if destination in ipv6_def then
    set local-preference 130
    set community VCNO_IPV6 additive
    done
  endif
  set local-preference 130
  set community VCNO_IPV6 additive
end-policy

route-policy PNI_TZL1_MICROSOFT_IMPORT_V4
  #REJECT BOGONS_V4
  if destination in BOGONS_V4 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_LONG_AS_PATH
  if as-path length ge 50 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT INVALID RPKI
  if validation-state is invalid then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT DEFAULT
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_BEGIN ###########################################
  #ACCEPT ROUTES BY AS-PATH&PREFIXES
  if destination in PNI_TZL1_MICROSOFT_PREFIXES_V4 and as-path in ASN_MICROSOFT then
    set local-preference 170
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    set community PNI_COMM additive
    done
  endif
  ################################  EXCEPTIONS_END  ###########################################
  #REJECT OTHERS
  drop
end-policy

route-policy from_dora_telekom_tier1_import
  delete community all
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT TT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '9121.*') then
    drop
  endif
  #Accept-Route-sol 
  if destination in Accept-Dora-Telekom or as-path in (ios-regex '^48737_') then
    set local-preference 170
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    set community Dora_Telekom additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

    apply INTERNET_EXIT_TEST_SEABONE
    done
  elseif community matches-any OTHER_THAN_GECICI1_TUZLA_COMMUNITY then

    apply INTERNET_EXIT_TEST_SEABONE
    done
  else
    apply INTERNET_EXIT_TEST_SEABONE
  endif
  drop
end-policy

route-policy Magticom_Ipv4_Tuzlavf_BGP_IMPORT
  delete community all

    set community BGP-Customers additive
    set local-preference 140
    set community 6762:18612 additive
    set community 1273:18621 additive
    set community 6762:20302 additive
    done
  endif
  if destination in (213.157.222.0/24) then
    set local-preference 170
    set community Magticom additive
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    set community 1273:18622 additive
    set community 3356:15911 additive
    set community 1273:80 additive
    set community 3356:86 additive
    done
  endif
  if destination in Magticom_Ipv4_Prefixes then
    set local-preference 170
    set community Magticom additive
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    set community 1273:18621 additive
    set community 1273:15722 additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

!
route-policy Medianova_Mednautilus_BGP_Export
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY
  if community matches-any VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #TNAP REJECT
  if community matches-any TIER1-GLOBAL-COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  # VFNET_ERLAB
  if destination in (212.15.16.0/20) then
    done
  endif
  #VF_Mobil_Prefixes
  if community matches-any ANK_BOLGE_BGP_CUSTOMERS or community matches-any IST_AND_BGP_CUSTOMERS then
    done
  endif
  # VFNET_DSL_INJECTION
  if destination in (81.8.82.0/24, 95.65.252.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #SPESIFIK_ANONS_TO_SOL
  if destination in (82.150.93.0/24) then
    prepend as-path 15924 3
    done
  endif
  # VFNET-Anons-Spesifik
  if community matches-any VFNET-CAMLICA or community matches-any VFNet-Koza and destination in (193.243.192.0/19, 213.194.110.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #ofis_ipleri
  if destination in (213.194.95.0/24, 31.145.9.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #Reject-Term
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  #International-Pops
  if community matches-any International-Pops then
    drop
  endif
  #Network-Statements
  if community matches-any Bgp-Main-Network-Statements then
    done
  endif
  #Datacenter-Networks
  if community matches-any Dc-Blocks then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Bgp-Customers
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_allocations
  if community matches-any allocations then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #yurtici_blackhole
  if community matches-any TTNET-Sadece-yurtici then
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_primary
  if community matches-any announce_from_esentepe_atm then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_backup
  if community matches-any announce_from_esentepe_me or community matches-any announce_from_bostanci then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

route-policy SEABONE-BGP-TUZLA-PRIMARY-EXPORT
  #ONLY_ANNOUNCE_FROM_HERE
  if community matches-any DROP_COMM_ONLY_SEABONE_TUZLA_INT_PRI then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY
  if community matches-any VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #F5 CLOUD Service
  if community matches-any F5_CLOUD_DDOS_Servis_Anons_Kes or community matches-any F5_CLOUD_DDOS_ALWAYS_ON then
    drop
  endif
  #Only Announce TC Peering
  if community matches-any TC-Only then
    drop
  endif
  #BLACKHOLE
  if community matches-any VFNET-ARBOR-BLACKHOLE then
    set community VCNO-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community SEABONE-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community INTEROUTE-BLACKHOLE additive

    done

  if community matches-any VFNET_TT then
    prepend as-path 15924 2
    apply TT-BGP-TUZLA-INT-PRIMARY-EXPORT
    done
  elseif community matches-any OTHER_THAN_TT_PRIMARY_TUZLA_COMMUNITY then
    prepend as-path 15924 7
    apply TT-BGP-TUZLA-INT-PRIMARY-EXPORT
    done
  elseif community matches-any TT_PRIMARY_TUZLA_COMMUNITY_SECONDARY then
    prepend as-path 15924 4
    apply TT-BGP-TUZLA-INT-PRIMARY-EXPORT
    done
  else
    apply TT-BGP-TUZLA-INT-PRIMARY-EXPORT
  endif
  drop
end-policy

route-policy TUZLA-Cloudfare-CDN-CACHING-BGP-EXPORT
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any DO-NOT-ANNOUNCE-TNAP then
    drop
  endif
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^6762_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT TT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^9121_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT INTEROUTE PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^8928_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT Superonline PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^34984_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT VCNO IP TRANSIT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^1273_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT LEVEL3 IP TRANSIT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^3356_') then
    drop
  endif
  #TNAP REJECT
  if community matches-any TIER1-GLOBAL-COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #Drop2Cloudfare_PNI
  if community matches-any DROP_Cloudfare_PNI then
    drop
  endif
  #VODAFONE_MOBILE
  if community matches-any VF-GZM-vGGSN05 then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    done
  endif
  #ULAKBIM  
  if community matches-any Ulakbim then
    done
  endif
  #VFNET BIRI PREFIXES
  if community matches-any VFNET_BODRUMISG then
    done
  endif
  #VFNET
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^$') then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

    done

    done
  endif

    set community Customer-Voice-Subnetted additive
  endif
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    set next-hop self
    done
  endif

    drop
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any TTNET_TUZLA then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VCNO_TUZLA then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any NSU_IPBB_GNS_1 or community matches-any NSU_IPBB_GNS_2 or community matches-any NSU_IPBB_TZL_1 or community matches-any NSU_IPBB_TZL_2 then
    done

end-policy

route-policy IBGP-EXPORT-TO-INTERNET-ROUTERS-FOR-IPv6
  #IP_Transit_Ipv6_Prefixes
  if community matches-any VCNO_IPV6 or community matches-any SEABONE_IPV6 then
    done
  endif
  #Peering_Ipv6_Prefixes
  if community matches-any tier1_global_community then
    done
  endif
  #Internet_Customers_Ipv6_Prefixes
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    set next-hop self
    done
  endif
  if destination in Ipv6_IntRouter_Loopbacks_Range then
    drop
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

    done

end-policy
